< Review>
Duke Bakery is unique for their breads stuffed with goodies on the inside.   I love that they have samples for most of their breads because the sizes are not individually portioned; it's still good the second day.   Commitment is easier once you know you want to indulge in a particular flavor. The breads are consistently soft and fluffy.  Our default choices are strawberry milk, taro angel, and choco & blue mt. coffee.  They rotate some flavors around and some sell out faster than others. Best bet is to go in the mornings for first picks.  Quick note about the milk tea - drink isn't great, but the boba is QQ; there are plenty of better options.

PS - the parking lot is usually packed; I'd avoid making a special trip during prime time dim sum hours.<//Review>

We brought him to you and you made sure he was neutered, vaccinated and flea treated. We were referred to another rescue and this rescue took the cat. The staff members were very nice and explained their position but it was hard to understand why cats could not be checked for socialization and put up for adoption. Young cats have a much better chance at adoption than cats over 6 months.<//Text>

<review>Trust is everything.

This evening was my first visit to, "Project Cannabis NoHo."
I am not a retail customer with fun wants, but a medicinal patient with actual needs---big difference.

I called, before visiting, so as to verify that they were a medical-grade facility with a consistent selection of flowers and inexpensive house/private reserve pre-rolls, which they confirmed.
I arrived to find a brightly-lit, busy, clean, efficiently-run, organized, tourist-friendly retail storefront (complete with branded apparel/merchandise), instead of a straightforward medical dispensary, intended for local patients.

The friendly representative, who assisted me, was the very individual, with whom, I spoke on the phone (all-the-more disappointing, when I realized the emphasis on our interaction was opting for completion of the transaction as quickly as possible, as opposed to taking seriously my medical needs/preferences as a patient).

They were out of the aforementioned (less expensive) pre-rolls, which was the main purpose for my visit, this evening.
Instead, I selected an inexpensive eighth and their last two single-gram (Indica) pre-rolls.
I got all of the way home to find that the eighth was too weak to be adequately effective, and they substituted a different (Hybrid) strain for one of my Indica pre-rolls without informing me.

A facility is only as good as its employees and/or its least expensive strain---if not good enough to represent your organization, then it should not be offered as such.

Special Note: Where I received a discount of $1.00 for my use of their recycled zip-top bag (which they provide to new customers), I did not receive any sort of raincheck (for the out-of-stock-items promised), or the customary new-patient-discount.

...again, trust is everything...
*pouting*<//review><pictures>None<//pictures><resp>None< /resp><Gmap_id>0x80c2958b7d4bd6b5:0x631d3d240404c008</Gmap_id></record>

<Rating>5< /Rating><Review>This place is amazing! I love Thai food and have eaten at many different places over the years and Thai-rriffic is one of the best! I moved to this area about six months ago and Thai-rriffic is just down the street. I have been wanting to go since the first time I saw their restaurant. I finally ordered takeout last night and I am so upset with myself for not going there sooner. I got the Pahd Thai with tofu because it is my fave Thai dish so I judge all Thai restaurants by how they make it. If they can't make Pad Thai right, then I don't go back. The Pad Thai sauce was flavored differently than what I'm used to but it was absolutely amazing! And even though the food was in a paper box they had still taken the time to garnish it beautifully. I also got their Sweet Potato appetizer. Oh my! What a treat for the taste buds! This dish is sweet potato slices dipped in coconut and sesame batter and fried. The batter was light and airy and was fried to perfection. Each piece was golden brown and the sweet potato slice inside was perfectly tender. They are served with what they call a pickled chili-cucumber-peanut relish. The relish is more of a clear thin tangy sauce with small pieces of cucumber, finely chopped peanuts, and a small spoonful of chili sauce layered on top so you can mix according to taste. My tastebuds came alive with the first taste of this delightful sauce. It is one of the most delicious things I have ever tasted. The spice and tang of the relish pairs perfectly with the sweetness of the sweet potatoes. I cannot recommend this appetizer enough. Though I must warn you that you will grieve when the last piece is gone. If you eat at Thai-rriffic without ordering the sweet potatoes, you have truly done yourself a disservice. In addition to some of the best Thai food I have ever had the pleasure of consuming, I will return to Thai-rriffic for the service and atmosphere. The gentleman who took my order was very friendly and helpful. He said my order would be ready in fifteen minutes but it was much quicker than that. Their dining area is quaint and cozy and would make a lovely place to enjoy a long leisurely meal and conversation with your favorite dinner dates.</Review><gmapID>0x80ecf0e1600e8885:0x428c7f40e5787d07< /gmapID>< UserId.>

<time>1600833271178</time><Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
I have eaten at many different Del Tacos for the past 40+ years. Sometimes 7 days a week, sometimes just a couple days a week. This one has become my favorite. The food proportions are always about what their menu states them to be. Many other Del Tacos have been skimping, for example, Seal Beach Blvd Del Taco 1/2 lb bean and cheese burritos weighing under 5oz, that‚Äôs with 2 scoops of guacamole added. Multiple times. Other locations doing the same. This location on Western does not skimp. The food is always fresh and the fries are USUALLY hot, sometimes warm, but USUALLY hot. Every staff member I‚Äôve interacted with actually listens while your are placing your order and also at the window. When I answer ‚Äòno‚Äô to the sauce question, they don‚Äôt ask 3 or 4 times, they ask once. And they don‚Äôt dump a huge handful of sauces and ketchup in the bag like so many of the other locations do even after I answered no multiple times. It is refreshing to go to a business where the people actually care about serving the customer. FYI, I only go to this location before noon, so I haven‚Äôt had the pleasure of dealing with the night staff.< /Review>
